[17:27:49] #staff <Rubikon>: —è –≤ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω–µ—Ç–µ –Ω–∞—à–µ–ª —Ç–∞–∫—É—é —à—Ç—É–∫—É ```python@bot.command(name='gdq')
async def gdq(ctx):
    #GDQ Date
    gdq_date = datetime.datetime(2020, 8, 16, 18, 30)
    qdelta = gdq_date - datetime.datetime.now().replace(microsecond=0)

    def strfdelta(delta, fmt):
        d = {"days": delta.days}
        d["hours"], rem = divmod(delta.seconds, 3600)
        d["minutes"], d["seconds"] = divmod(rem, 60)
        return fmt.format(**d)

    print('SGDQ 2020 starts in:', strfdelta(qdelta, f"{days} days, {hours} hours,"
                                                    f" {minutes} minutes, 'and', {seconds} seconds"))
    await ctx.send('SGDQ 2020 starts in: ', strfdelta(qdelta, f"{days} days, {hours} hours, "
                                                              f"{minutes} minutes, 'and', {seconds} seconds"))
```

[18:51:38] #staff <Rubikon>: ```python
@bot.command(name='steam_player', help='shows real name and full avatar of given user')
async def game_news(ctx, steam_url: str):
    x = []
    if ',' in steam_url:
        names = steam_url.split(',')
        print(names)
        for name in names:
            steamids = steam.steamid.steam64_from_url(f'https://steamcommunity.com/id/{name}')
            x.append(requests.get(f'https://api.steampowered.com/ISteamUser/GetPlayerSummaries/v0002/?key={STEAM_KEY}&format=json&steamids={steamids}'))
    elif 'steamcommunity.com' in steam_url:
        steamids = steam.steamid.steam64_from_url('https://steamcommunity.com/id/{}'.format(re.findall("\\w*$", steam_url)[0]))
        print(steamids)
        x.append(requests.get(f'https://api.steampowered.com/ISteamUser/GetPlayerSummaries/v0002/?key={STEAM_KEY}&format=json&steamids={steamids}'))
    else:
        steamids = steam.steamid.steam64_from_url(f'https://steamcommunity.com/id/{steam_url}')
        x.append(requests.get(f'https://api.steampowered.com/ISteamUser/GetPlayerSummaries/v0002/?key={STEAM_KEY}&format=json&steamids={steamids}'))

    for user in x:
        print(f"Real name: {user.json()['response']['players'][0]['realname']} \n"
              f"Full avatar link: {user.json()['response']['players'][0]['avatarfull']}")
        await ctx.send(f"Real name: {user.json()['response']['players'][0]['realname']} \n"
                       f"Full avatar link: {user.json()['response']['players'][0]['avatarfull']}")
```
